## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Script as ReplayScript
    participant DB as Database
    participant AWS as AWS_Lambdas
    participant Trip as TripLegService
    participant Ent as EntityService
    participant Helper as Helpers
    participant SNS as SNS_Topic

    ReplayScript->>DB: SELECT position_update records between from_time and to_time
    DB-->>ReplayScript: rows (records)
    loop for each record
        alt record.trip_leg_id present
            ReplayScript->>DB: SELECT actual_trip_leg JOIN solution WHERE id=record.trip_leg_id
            DB-->>ReplayScript: trip_leg row
            ReplayScript->>AWS: get_sample_admin_event(http_method='GET', solutions=[trip_leg.solution_id], customer_id=trip_leg.customer_id)
            AWS-->>ReplayScript: event
            ReplayScript->>Trip: process_position_request(event, solution_id, body, transport_mode, location_ids)
            Trip-->>ReplayScript: request
            ReplayScript->>DB: set_location_on_position_update -> UPDATE position_update (if location_code or changed position_type)
            DB-->>ReplayScript: update ack
            ReplayScript->>DB: get_entities_on_trip_leg(...)
            DB-->>ReplayScript: ext_entity_ids
            ReplayScript->>SNS: send_to_entity_position_updated_sns_topic(ext_entity_ids, solution_id)
            SNS-->>ReplayScript: ack
            alt request.references present
                ReplayScript->>DB: add_position_update_references(position_update_id, references, actual_trip_leg_id)
                DB-->>ReplayScript: ack
            end
        else record.entity_id present
            ReplayScript->>DB: SELECT active_entity JOIN solution WHERE ae.id=record.entity_id
            DB-->>ReplayScript: entity row
            ReplayScript->>AWS: get_sample_admin_event(http_method='GET', solutions=[entity.solution_id], customer_id=entity.customer_id)
            AWS-->>ReplayScript: event
            ReplayScript->>Ent: process_position_request(event, cursor, solution_id, ext_entity_id, entity_internal_id, body)
            Ent-->>ReplayScript: request
            alt request.source_type == PositionUpdate.SourceType.DEFAULT
                ReplayScript->>Helper: get_custom_connected_car_position_type(cursor, request.position_type, entity.solution_id)
                Helper-->>ReplayScript: custom_position_type
            end
            ReplayScript->>DB: set_location_on_position_update -> UPDATE position_update (if location_code or changed position_type)
            DB-->>ReplayScript: update ack
            ReplayScript->>SNS: send_to_entity_position_updated_sns_topic([entity.external_id], solution_id)
            SNS-->>ReplayScript: ack
            alt request.references present
                ReplayScript->>DB: add_position_update_references(position_update_id, references, entity_id)
                DB-->>ReplayScript: ack
            end
        end
    end
```
